window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

           <div class="modules-membercenter-about-me " data-ox-name="modules.membercenter.AboutMe" data-ox-context="MemberCenter_ProfileData, Errors, Member"> 
            <div class="aboutMe profileBox">
             <span class="header">About Me</span> 
             <div class="info">
              <p>Since Jul 2006</p>
              <p>Lives in Richmond, Virginia</p>
              <p> Female </p>
              <p>Ia Orana (Hello in Tahitian) The minute I set foot on a French Polynesian Island in 2005 I knew this was going to be my place. I have traveled throughout the world since I was 16, have been to many islands in the Caribbean and other places in the world but nothing compares to the beauty of Tahiti and her Islands. Since 2005 I have traveled to French Polynesia multiple times visiting and staying at many resorts. I have lived and worked in Moorea for several months getting further immersed in the Tahitian culture and customs. I am certified with the Tahiti Tourist board, and owner of Crossroads Travel Inc, established in 1983 and a member of Virtuoso. Mauru'uru Roa for stopping by to check out my profile Regards Bo (Uschi) uschi@crttravel.com 804 794-7700 www.crttravel.com Uschi Helfrich </p>
             </div>
            </div> 
           </div>
